# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="e4331-102">.NET Framework'teki eski türler</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e4331-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="e4331-103">Bu makaledeki tablolar, artık kullanılmayan türler listesinde [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] ve [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], derleme tarafından düzenlenmiş.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e4331-103">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e4331-104">Eski türler ve önerilen alternatifleri her derlemede bir listesini görmek için aşağıdaki bağlantıları kullanın.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e4331-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e4331-105">Bu tür geçersiz olduğundan, tüm üyeleri de artık kullanılmıyor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e4331-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e4331-106">.NET Framework Sınıf Kitaplığı'nda ek eski üyeler listesi için bkz. [eski üyeler](obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e4331-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](obsolete-members.md).</span></span>
